<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自适应网格细化（AMR）的效率不仅取决于细化算法本身，还高度依赖于标记单元的策略及其调优方式，然而目前缺乏对不同标记策略的系统性比较研究，尤其是统计方法的潜力尚未被充分评估。

Method: 以残差驱动的Kelly误差估计器为基础，在稳态固体和流体力学问题上，对比了经典标记方法（最大值法、Dörfler bulk-chasing法、分位数法）与非经典统计方法（z-score法、Isolation Forest法）的性能。

Result: 分位数法和z-score法在各种问题中表现出最稳定的鲁棒性；Dörfler法在较大bulk参数时效果好；最大值法对不规则场敏感；Isolation Forest在宽松的contamination参数下可媲美顶级经典方法，但在激进设置下表现不佳。

Conclusion: 研究结果为实际自适应FEM工作流中选择平衡细化激进程度与计算成本的标记策略提供了实践指导。

Abstract: Adaptive mesh refinement (AMR) is indispensable for efficient finite element analyses. However, its performance depends not only on the refinement itself but also on strategy to mark elements for refinement and the way it is tuned. This work compares classical marking methods (maximum, Dörfler bulk-chasing, quantile) with non-classical, statistically based approaches (z-score, Isolation Forest), all driven by the residual-based Kelly error estimator and tested on steady solid and fluid mechanics problems. The study finds quantile and z-score markings to be the most robust, Dörfler effective for large bulk parameters, and maximum marking sensitive to irregular fields. Isolation Forest can rival top classical methods with a generous contamination level but may fail under aggressive settings. These results offer practical guidance for selecting marking strategies that balance refinement aggressiveness and computational cost in adaptive FEM workflows.

</details>


### [258] [Scenario-driven optimization of passive vehicle suspensions: explaining the effectiveness of asymmetric damping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05235)
*José Geraldo Telles Ribeiro,Americo Cunha*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于场景驱动的优化框架，系统推导了非对称阻尼在车辆悬架中的有效性。使用四分之一车辆模型和ISO 8608道路激励，通过交叉熵算法优化回弹与压缩阻尼比。结果表明：中等激励下对称阻尼通常足够，而强烈激励下非对称阻尼才显必要，传统2-3倍回弹/压缩比只是特定场景下的近似最优解，而非普适常数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非对称阻尼（回弹阻尼通常推荐为压缩阻尼的2-3倍）在被动悬架中广泛应用，但这一准则长期基于经验而缺乏基于车辆动力学和激励条件的系统推导。作者旨在提供一个原理性的解释框架来证明非对称阻尼的有效性。

Method: 采用最小化四分之一车辆模型，将回弹和压缩阻尼比作为独立设计变量；使用标准化ISO 8608道路激励；通过随机交叉熵算法对基于仿真的非凸目标函数进行优化；性能评估指标包括ISO 2631加权RMS加速度、轮胎-地面接触力变异性和稳定时间。

Result: 对称阻尼在中等激励下通常足够；非对称阻尼仅在强烈激励条件下才变得必要；传统推荐的2-3倍回弹/压缩比并非普适常数，而是依赖于具体场景的近似最优解。

Conclusion: 该研究为非对称阻尼的经验准则提供了系统性的动力学解释，明确了其适用条件与场景依赖性，有助于更理性地设计车辆悬架阻尼比。

Abstract: Asymmetric damping is widely used in passive vehicle suspensions, with rebound damping often recommended to exceed compression damping by a factor of two to three. Despite its prevalence, this guideline remains largely empirical and lacks a systematic derivation based on vehicle dynamics and excitation conditions. This paper presents a scenario-driven optimization framework that provides a principled explanation for the effectiveness of asymmetric damping. A minimal quarter-car model is employed to isolate the key mechanisms governing the trade-off between ride comfort, road holding, and transient response, using standardized ISO~8608 road excitations. Rebound and compression damping ratios are treated as independent design variables, and optimal configurations are identified via a stochastic Cross-Entropy algorithm applied to a non-convex, simulation-based objective function. Performance is assessed through ISO~2631 weighted RMS acceleration, tire--ground contact force variability, and settling time. The results show that symmetric damping is often sufficient under moderate excitation, whereas asymmetric damping becomes necessary under severe conditions, with commonly cited rebound-to-compression ratios emerging as scenario-dependent near-optimal solutions rather than universal constants.

</details>


### [259] [A Comparison of Massively Parallel Performance Portable Particle-in-Cell schemes for electrostatic kinetic plasma simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05469)
*Sonali Mayani,Paul Fischill,Sriramkrishnan Muralikrishnan,Andreas Adelmann*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文在静电Vlasov-Poisson系统背景下，比较了FFT伪谱求解器、矩阵自由有限差分PCG求解器、矩阵自由有限元求解器以及粒子-傅里叶（PIF）方案等不同的泊松求解器。实验在多种GPU架构（AMD和Nvidia）上进行，以Landau阻尼为基准测试。结果表明FFT求解器在绝对时间上最优但适用性有限；其他PIC求解器耗时高一个量级但可扩展性相似；PIF方案作为高保真替代方案，虽比FFT方案昂贵但展现出优异的可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在静电Vlasov-Poisson系统中，不同的泊松求解器在性能、可移植性和适用性方面存在显著差异，需要系统性的比较研究来指导不同计算场景下的求解器选择。

Method: 基于IPPL库实现了FFT伪谱求解器、矩阵自由有限差分PCG求解器、矩阵自由FEM求解器和PIF方案，在512^3和1024^3网格尺寸、每单元8粒子的设置下，以Landau阻尼为基准，在AMD GPU（LUMI）和Nvidia GPU（Alps、JUWELS Booster）上进行性能对比。

Result: FFT求解器在绝对计算时间上最优但适用性受限；PCG和FEM等PIC求解器耗时高一个量级但可扩展性与FFT相当；PIF方案作为高保真替代方案，虽比FFT-PIC方案更昂贵，但在所有架构上均展现出优异的可扩展性。

Conclusion: FFT求解器适用于对计算时间敏感且问题适用的情况；PIC方案中的其他场求解器在可扩展性上可接受但成本较高；PIF方案在保真度和可扩展性间取得了良好平衡，是多架构高性能计算场景下极具潜力的选择。

Abstract: We compare different Poisson solvers within the context of an electrostatic Vlasov-Poisson system. These schemes are implemented as part of the IPPL (Independent Parallel Particle Layer) library (Frey et al., 2024), which provides performance portable and dimension independent building blocks for scientific simulations requiring particle-mesh methods, with Eulerian (mesh-based) and Lagrangian (particle-based) approaches. The simulation used to compare the performance and portability of the schemes is Landau damping, part of a set of mini-applications implemented to benchmark and showcase the capabilities of the IPPL library (Muralikrishnan et al., 2024). We use grid-sizes of $512^3$ and $1024^3$ with 8 particles per cell, running with different algorithms in the solve phase of the Particle-in-Cell (PIC) loop: a Fast Fourier Transform (FFT) pseudo-spectral solver, a matrix-free finite difference Preconditioned Conjugate Gradient (PCG) solver, and a matrix-free Finite Element (FEM) solver. We also compare these PIC schemes to the novel Particle-in-Fourier (PIF) scheme, which performs interpolations using non-uniform FFTs thereby avoiding a grid in the real space. We obtain results on different computing architectures, such as AMD GPUs (LUMI at CSC), and Nvidia GPUs (Alps at CSCS and JUWELS Booster at Jülich Supercomputing Center), showcasing portability. In terms of absolute time the FFT solver is advantageous, but is limited in its applicability. All other field solvers in the PIC scheme are an order-of-magnitude more expensive in terms of time, but scale similarly to the FFT case in the electrostatic PIC context. The PIF scheme serves as a high fidelity alternative to standard PIC, and while it is costlier than the FFT-based PIC scheme, it shows excellent scalability on all the architectures.

</details>


### [260] [Discrete Elastic Ribbons: A Unified Discrete Differential Geometry Framework for One-Dimensional Energy Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05529)
*Shivam Kumar Panda,M Khalid Jawed*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于离散微分几何的统一仿真框架，用于比较五种弹性带（ribbon）模型（Kirchhoff、Sadowsky、Wunderlich、Sano、Audoly），发现Sano模型在捕捉宽度相关的分叉阈值方面与壳单元有限元仿真最为接近，且计算开销与标准DER相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于中心线的带模型试图通过耦合弯扭能量捕捉宽度依赖性，但由于缺乏统一的仿真框架，其相对精度尚不明确。

Method: 基于离散微分几何，将能量表示为沿中心线的耦合弯扭应变度量函数（而非DER中二次弯扭能量的线性求和），推导了解析梯度和海森矩阵以实现隐式时间积分；在统一框架下比较了五种带模型，并以预屈曲拱的横向加载超临界叉形分叉作为基准，与壳单元有限元仿真对比。

Result: Sano模型在捕捉宽度依赖的分叉阈值方面与壳单元有限元仿真最为接近；基于JAX的高性能实现达到了O(N)的每迭代计算成本，且Sano模型相比标准DER每迭代开销可忽略不计。

Conclusion: Sano模型是现有中心线带模型中捕捉宽度效应的最优选择，且计算效率高，适合大规模仿真。

Abstract: Elastic ribbons, slender structures whose length ($L$), width ($W$), and thickness ($b$) satisfy $L \gg W \gg b$, exhibit mechanical behaviors intermediate between one-dimensional rods ($L \gg W, b$) and two-dimensional plates ($L, W \gg b$). In quadratic Kirchhoff-type rod-based frameworks, such as Discrete Elastic Rods (DER), the governing equilibrium equations are independent of width, and therefore these models cannot capture width-dependent mechanical effects. Reduced centerline-based ribbon models attempt to capture width dependence via coupled bending-twisting energies. However, their relative accuracy remain unclear due to the absence of a unified simulation framework. In this work, we formulate a framework grounded in discrete differential geometry where the energy is expressed as functions of coupled bending-twisting strain measures along the centerline, rather than a linear sum of quadratic bending and twisting energies in DER. We derive analytical gradients and Hessians of the energy that enable implicit time integration. Within this unified setting, we compare five ribbon models: Kirchhoff, Sadowsky, Wunderlich, Sano, and Audoly. As a benchmark, a straight ribbon is longitudinally constrained into a pre-buckled arch and subjected to transverse displacement, inducing a supercritical pitchfork bifurcation. Predicted bifurcation thresholds are compared against shell-based finite element simulations, with the Sano model providing the closest agreement in capturing width-dependent shifts. Our high-performance JAX-based implementation achieves $\mathcal{O}(N)$ per-iteration cost and also confirms that Sano model introduces negligible per-iteration overhead relative to standard DER.

</details>


### [261] [Quantum Optimization for Electromagnetics: Physics-Informed QAOA for Reconfigurable Intelligent Surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06048)
*Marco Pasquale,Erik M. Åsgrim,Stefano Markidis,Oscar Quevedo-Teruel*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文研究了在含噪中等规模量子（NISQ）设备上，通过将渐进式物理模型（互耦合）嵌入QUBO公式来优化可重构智能表面（RIS），发现全局耦合虽能最大化波束赋形精度，但稀疏距离惩罚模型是当前量子硬件可行的必要折中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前量子算法优化RIS时忽略互耦合等物理约束，导致实际性能严重下降；需要探索在量子计算框架中融入物理信息模型的可能性与可行性。

Method: 将渐进式物理信息互耦合模型嵌入QUBO公式，针对5×5网格评估四种Ising相互作用模型（从理想相位到全稠密物理模型），并采用QAOA进行优化。

Result: 全局耦合可最大化波束赋形精度，但稠密哈密顿量引入过高的路由开销并影响收敛；稀疏距离惩罚模型在精度与硬件可行性间取得平衡。

Conclusion: 物理信息量子优化在数学上可行，但在当前NISQ设备上，必须采用稀疏距离惩罚模型作为必要折中方案。

Abstract: Optimizing Reconfigurable Intelligent Surfaces (RIS) is a high-dimensional combinatorial challenge. Current quantum algorithms often simplify this problem by ignoring physical constraints like mutual coupling, which significantly degrades real-world performance. Rather than targeting a fully realistic RIS description, we embed progressively more physics-informed models of mutual coupling into Quadratic Unconstrained Binary Optimization (QUBO) formulations. We evaluate four Ising interaction models ($J_{ij}$) for the Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm (QAOA), ranging from idealized phase-only to fully dense physical models. Analyzing a $5 \times 5$ grid, our results expose a critical trade-off between spatial pointing accuracy and quantum hardware feasibility. While complete global coupling maximizes beamforming precision, dense Hamiltonians introduce prohibitive routing overhead and complicate convergence on near-term processors. Ultimately, we demonstrate that while physics-informed quantum optimization is mathematically viable, sparse, distance-penalized models remain a necessary compromise for execution on current noisy intermediate-scale quantum (NISQ) devices.

### [262] [Adaptive Coordinate Transforms for Neural Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06203)
*Chaoyu Liu,Zhonghao Li,Gaohang Chen,Zakhar Shumaylov,Zhongying Deng,Qian Zhang,Zhonghua Qiao,Carola-Bibiane Schönlieb*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 提出自适应坐标变换（ACT）模块，通过可微采样学习数据驱动的坐标变换，解决神经算子中固定欧拉坐标与动态物理结构之间的空间错配问题，显著提升多种PDE基准上的预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经算子在固定欧拉坐标下处理PDE，静态坐标与演化物理结构之间存在空间错配，导致非必要的非局部算子映射并强化了陡峭过渡区域的平滑偏好，限制了模型性能。

Method: 设计ACT模块作为即插即用组件：输入特征后学习坐标变换，通过可微采样在变换坐标下重新表示同一特征，保持底层信号的同时改变空间表征，实现对数据自适应的几何调整。

Result: 在多种PDE基准和多种神经算子架构上，ACT模块均带来一致且显著的预测精度提升。

Conclusion: 学习自适应坐标系统是增强神经算子学习的有效机制，能够更好地跟踪演化结构、降低算子复杂度并动态聚焦关键特征。

Abstract: Neural operators have achieved promising performance on partial differential equations (PDEs), but most existing models are built on fixed Eulerian coordinates. This mismatch between evolving physical structures and static coordinates creates spatial misalignment, leading to unnecessarily non-local operator mappings and reinforcing a smoothness preference near sharp transitions. Inspired by adaptive coordinate transformations in classical PDE analysis, we propose the Adaptive Coordinate Transform (ACT) block, a plug-and-play module for data-driven geometric adaptation in neural operators. ACT blocks resolve this structural limitation by learning adaptive coordinate systems within the operator learning pipeline. Specifically, given an input feature, the ACT block learns a coordinate transformation and represents the same feature under the transformed coordinates via differentiable sampling. This operation preserves the underlying signal while changing its spatial representation, equivalent to expressing the same physical quantity in different coordinate systems. By adapting the coordinate system to the data, ACT allows the network to better track evolving structures, reduce operator complexity, and dynamically focus on critical features to improve learning. We evaluate the proposed approach across diverse PDE benchmarks and multiple neural operator architectures. Experimental results demonstrate consistent and significant improvements in predictive accuracy, indicating that learning coordinate systems provides a powerful mechanism for enhancing operator learning.

</details>

### [263] [On Unbiased Parameter Estimation and Signal Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05276)
*Joonas Lahtinen*

Main category: cs.IT

Method: 推导无噪声条件下可恢复参数数量的上界，定义概率测度来评估正确恢复所有非零参数及其幅值顺序的概率，从数学角度分析噪声鲁棒性。

Result: 给出了无噪声条件下可恢复参数数量的理论上界；建立了概率测度框架；数学解释了无偏与标准化方法的噪声鲁棒性；揭示了传感器数量与信噪比之间的权衡关系。

Conclusion: 成功将深度无偏源定位理论扩展到一般性参数估计问题，为理解无偏与标准化方法的噪声性能提供了数学基础，并发现了传感器数量与信噪比之间的关键权衡。

Abstract: In this paper, we expand the theory of depth-unbiased source localization to unbiased parameter estimation and signal reconstruction of an arbitrary number of non-zero parameters to be recovered. The topic touches on the concept of exact reconstructibility, most commonly known in compressed sensing and multisource estimation in various imaging problems. The theoretical results derive upper bounds on the number of recoverable parameters in the noiseless case, and a probability measure is defined to assess the probability of obtaining all non-zero parameters with correct magnitude order. The work provides a mathematical explanation of the open question regarding the noise robustness of standardized and unbiased methods. Also, the paper reveals a trade-off between the number of sensors and the signal-to-noise ratio. Numerical experiments demonstrate the theoretical findings.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出多任务语义自编码器联合重构与标签预测；建立潜在维度作为跨层控制变量的延迟-语义保真度权衡模型；设计队列感知的漂移加罚策略（最小化延迟）和年龄感知策略（最小化平均信息年龄），两者均在长期语义错误约束下在线调整语义速率。

Conclusion: 通过在线调整潜在维度自适应语义速率，可有效平衡语义保真度与延迟/信道资源，提升无线语义通信系统的频谱效率和时效性。

Abstract: Semantic communication (SemCom) with learned encoder-decoder architectures enables end-to-end learning of compact task-oriented representations optimized for the wireless channel, reducing channel resources needed to convey task-relevant information and improving spectrum efficiency. This paper studies semantic image transmission over block Rayleigh fading with AWGN using a multi-task semantic autoencoder that jointly reconstructs images and predicts labels from the received waveform. The latent dimension (complex channel uses per source sample) serves as a cross-layer control variable governing semantic fidelity and channel resource usage. We characterize the resulting latency-task fidelity tradeoff: larger latent representations improve inference accuracy but increase service time, channel uses, and queueing delay. Building on this insight, we develop online semantic-rate controllers that adapt the latent dimension per update under a long-term semantic error constraint. A queue-aware drift-plus-penalty policy minimizes delay subject to an average semantic error cap, while a complementary age-aware policy minimizes time-average Age of Information (AoI). By adapting the semantic rate to congestion and fidelity requirements, the proposed framework improves spectrum utilization and enables timely semantic updates with significantly lower delay and AoI than fixed-rate baselines.

### [265] [Infinite families of constacyclic codes supporting 3-designs and their applications in coding theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05613)
*Hongsheng Hu,Nian Li,Yanan Wu,Xiangyong Zeng*

Method: 构造了两类无限族的λ-常循环码（在\mathbb{F}_{q^2}上），完全确定其参数和重量分布，进而研究子域子码，并应用于构造纠缠辅助量子纠错码和局部可恢复码。

Abstract: Constacyclic codes over finite fields are of theoretical importance as they are closely related to a number of areas of mathematics such as algebra, algebraic geometry, graph theory,
  combinatorial designs and number theory. However, the study of constacyclic codes in this context remains limited compared to classical cyclic codes. This paper provides two infinite families of $λ$-constacyclic codes over $\mathbb{F}_{q^2}$ that support infinite families of 3-designs, which generalize the results in [IEEE Trans. Inf. Theory 69(4): 2341-2354, 2023]. The parameters and weight distributions are determined completely. Besides, we study their subfield subcodes and applications on constructing entanglement-assisted quantum error-correcting codes (EAQECCs) and locally recoverable codes (LRCs). It is worthy to mention that two classes of maximal entanglement EAQECCs with a negative or a high positive net rate are derived. Moreover, two classes of distance-optimal and dimension-optimal LRCs are also obtained.

</details>


### [266] [An Additive Approximation Scheme for Generating Dyadic Codings for the Outputs of an LLM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05837)
*Daniella Bar-Lev,Farzad Farnoud,Ryan Gabrys*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究在编码速率约束下，用二叉树诱导的二元分布逼近离散概率分布（如LLM的下一个token分布）的问题，提出了多项式时间可加近似方案，并应用于LLM隐写术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 如何在给定编码速率约束下，用二叉树诱导的二元分布（dyadic distribution）最优地逼近一个离散概率分布（如大语言模型的next-token分布），以最小化总变差距离。

Method: 将该问题形式化为基于树的划分问题，并在常数速率条件下提出了一个多项式时间的加性近似方案（additive approximation scheme）。

Result: 证明了在速率约束下能够获得接近最优的二元逼近，并给出了可证明的保证。

Conclusion: 该框架为基于LLM的隐写术提供了理论基础，其中速率映射为每token嵌入的隐藏信息比特数，总变差界控制统计可检测性。

Abstract: We study the problem of approximating a discrete probability distribution, such as the next-token distribution of a large language model, by a dyadic distribution induced by a binary tree under encoding rate constraints. The objective is to partition the support of the distribution and assign dyadic probabilities to minimize total variation distance while achieving a prescribed rate. We formulate this task as a tree-based partitioning problem and develop a polynomial-time additive approximation scheme for the rate-constrained setting in the constant-rate regime. Our results provide provable guarantees for near-optimal dyadic approximations and, as an application, yield a principled framework for LLM-based steganography, where the rate maps to bits of hidden information embedded per token and the total variation bound controls statistical detectability.

</details>


### [267] [Identification for Inverse Gaussian Channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06103)
*Mohammad Javad Salariseddigh*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文推导了逆高斯信道（分子通信基础模型）在峰值时间约束下采用确定性编码方案的辨识容量上下界，发现其码本规模呈超指数增长～2^{(n log n)R}。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为流体环境中分子通信系统建立辨识容量的理论基础，揭示其相比于传统通信信道的容量增长特性。

Method: 基于逆高斯信道模型，考虑分子通过扩散和漂移到达接收器的随机首次到达时间噪声，在峰值时间约束下分析确定性编码方案，推导辨识容量的上下界。

Result: 在噪声的温和正则条件下，辨识容量呈超指数增长，码字长度n下的码本规模为～2^{(n log n)R}，其中R为编码速率。

Conclusion: 逆高斯信道在辨识框架下具有远超传统指数级容量的超指数增长能力，为分子通信的高效编码设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We derive lower and upper bounds on the identification capacity of inverse Gaussian channels, a fundamental model for molecular communications in fluid environments. The analysis considers deterministic encoding schemes under a peak time constraint and characterizes the asymptotic growth of codebook sizes. A central result reveals that, under a mild regularity condition on the noise, i.e., the stochastic first arrival time of an information-carrying molecule propagating via diffusion and drift to the receiver, the identification capacity exhibits super-exponential growth in the codeword length, $n,$ i.e., $\sim 2^{(n \log n)R},$ where $R$ is the coding rate.

</details>


### [268] [Locally Repairable Codes with Availability via Elliptic Function Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06182)
*Junjie Huang,Chang-An Zhao*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文通过椭圆函数域上的普通椭圆曲线（而非超奇异椭圆曲线）构造了具有一个或两个恢复集的局部可修复码，获得了若干新的最优局部可修复码族（码长可达O(q+2√q)），并提出了利用椭圆函数域自同构群构造具有两个恢复集的局部可修复码的通用框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于超奇异椭圆曲线的最优局部可修复码构造中可用曲线种类有限，本文旨在利用具有更多有理点的普通椭圆曲线来拓宽可用于构造最优局部可修复码的曲线选择范围。

Method: 采用椭圆函数域上的普通椭圆曲线（具有大量有理点）替换传统的超奇异椭圆曲线；设计了一种确定函数e_i的新构造方法，并利用椭圆函数域的自同构群构建了具有两个恢复集的局部可修复码的通用框架。

Result: 获得了若干新的q元最优局部可修复码族，码长可达O(q+2√q)且具有灵活局部性；构造了具有两个恢复集的q²元局部可修复码族，码长O(q²+2q)，Singleton缺陷为O(2ℓ/(q²+2q-8ℓ))。

Conclusion: 本文工作拓宽了可用于构造最优局部可修复码的曲线选择；提出的通用框架可系统构造具有两个恢复集的局部可修复码，且通过超奇异与普通椭圆曲线均能获得新码族。

Abstract: Locally repairable codes with availability have become essential components in modern large-scale distributed cloud storage systems and numerous other applications. In this paper, we focus on the construction of locally repairable codes with one or two recovering sets via elliptic function fields. Prior pioneering work by Li et al. (IEEE Trans. Inf. Theory, vol. 65, no. 1, 2019) and Ma and Xing (J. Comb. Theory Ser. A., vol. 193, 2023) employed maximal supersingular elliptic curves to obtain several optimal (classical) locally repairable codes. In contrast, we consider ordinary elliptic curves with many rational points. This approach yields several new families of \(q\)-ary optimal locally repairable codes with length \(O(q+2\sqrt{q})\) and flexible locality. Consequently, our work broadens the selection of curves available for the construction of optimal locally repairable codes.
  Furthermore, we present a general framework for constructing locally repairable codes with two recovering sets via automorphism groups of elliptic function fields. To realize this framework, we devise a novel construction for determining the functions \(e_i\) in the construction of locally repairable codes. By employing both supersingular and ordinary elliptic curves, we obtain several families of locally repairable codes with two recovering sets. In particular, we construct a family of \(q^2\)-ary locally repairable codes with two recovering sets, achieving length \(O(q^2+2q)\) and Singleton-defect \(O\!\left(\frac{2\ell}{q^2+2q-8\ell}\right)\), where \(\ell \mid\mid q + 2\) with \(4\ell < q\).

</details>


### [269] [Fluid Antenna Systems Enabling 6G HRLLC With Port Switching Delay](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06275)
*Xusheng Zhu,Kai-Kit Wong,Hao Xu,Chenguang Rao,Hyundong Shin*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究流体天线系统(FAS)在超可靠低延迟通信(HRLLC)中的性能，通过建模空间相关性、端口切换延迟和有限块长编码的耦合效应，推导出平均BLER和可达速率的闭式表达式，严格证明了可靠性、可达速率和能量效率在端口维度上呈严格单峰特性，并给出了FAS优于固定位置天线的切换延迟阈值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: FAS通过天线位置可重构性实现了紧凑外形下的 massive 空间分集，是6G用户终端的有前景技术。然而实际端口切换会引入延迟和信令开销，这在有限块长操作下对HRLLC尤为不利。现有研究缺乏对空间相关性、端口切换延迟和有限块长编码三者耦合效应的联合分析。

Method: 推导了空间相关衰落信道下平均BLER和平均可达速率的精确闭式表达式；通过理论分析证明可靠性、可达速率和能量效率在端口维度上严格单峰；刻画了区分FAS是否优于固定位置天线的切换延迟阈值。

Result: 增加端口数量提升分集增益但线性减少有效块长，加剧有限块长惩罚；三个关键性能指标在端口维度上严格单峰，存在唯一最优端口配置；当切换延迟低于推导的阈值时，FAS可获得显著的HRLLC性能增益。

Conclusion: FAS在HRLLC场景中能带来显著性能提升，但需在端口数目与切换延迟之间进行精细权衡，存在最优设计点；切换延迟阈值是决定FAS是否优于固定位置天线的关键判据。

Abstract: Fluid antenna systems (FAS) exploit antenna position reconfigurability to unlock massive spatial diversity within compact form factors, making them a promising enabler for 6G user terminals (UTs). However, practical port switching incurs latency and signaling overhead, which can be particularly detrimental to hyper-reliable low-latency communications (HRLLC) under finite blocklength operation. This paper investigates FASenabled HRLLC by explicitly capturing the coupled effects of spatial correlation, port switching delay, and finite blocklength coding. We derive exact closed-form expressions for the average block error rate (BLER) and average achievable rate over spatially correlated fading channels. The resulting analysis reveals a fundamental design trade-off: increasing the number of ports improves diversity but linearly reduces the effective blocklength, thereby intensifying finite-blocklength penalties. A key theoretical contribution is a rigorous proof that reliability, achievable rate, and energy efficiency are strictly unimodal in the port dimension, ensuring a unique optimal port configuration. Furthermore, we characterize an explicit switching-delay threshold that separates regimes where FAS yields net gains over fixed-position antenna (FPA) systems. Numerical results validate the analysis and show that substantial HRLLC performance gains are achievable when the switching latency remains below the derived bound.

</details>


### [270] [Affine Subcode Ensemble Decoding for Degeneracy-Aware Quantum Error Correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06547)
*Leo Wursthorn,Jonathan Mandelbaum,Sisi Miao,Hedongliang Liu,Holger Jäkel,Stergios Koutsioumpas,Laurent Schmalen*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出通过向稳定子码的校验矩阵添加线性无关行来减少退化解搜索空间，并将仿射子码集成解码技术从经典扩展到量子领域，在环面和广义自行车码上实现了更好的收敛性和更低的逻辑错误率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子低密度奇偶校验码的退化性会损害置信传播解码的收敛性，需要有效的解码方法来解决这一问题。

Method: 1) 向稳定子码的校验矩阵添加线性无关行以缩小退化解空间；2) 将仿射子码集成解码技术从经典扩展至量子场景；3) 为每条解码路径使用过完备矩阵。

Result: 蒙特卡洛模拟表明，在环面码和广义自行车码上，该方法改善了BP解码的收敛性并降低了逻辑错误率。

Conclusion: 所提方法有效缓解了量子LDPC码的退化性对BP解码的影响，为低开销容错量子计算提供了可行的解码方案。

Abstract: Quantum low-density parity-check codes are promising candidates for low-overhead fault-tolerant quantum computing, but degeneracy is known to impair the convergence of belief-propagation (BP) decoding of these codes. In this work, we show that appending linearly independent rows to a check matrix of a stabilizer code can reduce the search space for a valid degenerate solution. Motivated by this, we extend the recently proposed affine subcode ensemble decoding technique from the classical to the quantum setting. Moreover, we employ overcomplete matrices for each decoding path. Monte-Carlo simulations on toric and generalized bicycle codes demonstrate improved convergence and reduced logical error rate.

### [271] [Generalized Skew Multivariate Goppa Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06580)
*Elena Berardini,Pranav Trivedi*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文基于多变量Ore多项式理论，引入了广义斜多变量Goppa码，这类码包含广义斜Goppa码作为特例。通过提供新的校验矩阵，证明在某些假设下它们是广义斜Reed-Solomon码的子域子码，并给出了维数和最小距离的界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将斜Goppa码推广到多变量情形，并建立其与广义斜Reed-Solomon码的子域子码关系，以便更好地研究其参数性质。

Method: 利用多变量Ore多项式理论定义广义斜多变量Goppa码；构造新的校验矩阵；通过子域子码的视角建立与广义斜Reed-Solomon码的联系；推导维数和最小距离的界。

Result: 提出了广义斜多变量Goppa码；证明了广义斜Goppa码在特定条件下是广义斜Reed-Solomon码的子域子码；给出了维数和最小距离的界限。

Conclusion: 该工作将斜Goppa码推广到多变量情形，并利用子域子码关系为参数分析提供了理论工具。

Abstract: We introduce Generalized Skew Multivariate Goppa codes relying on the theory of multivariate Ore polynomials. These codes contain, as a particular case, the Generalized Skew Goppa codes. By providing a new parity check matrix for the latter, we show that, under some hypotheses, they are subfield subcodes of Generalized Skew Reed--Solomon codes. This result turns out to be helpful to study the parameters of Skew Multivariate Goppa codes, for which we provide bounds on their dimension and minimum distance.

</details>
